China National Aviation Corporation Increases Flights on Shanghai-Hankou Route and Changes Flight Schedule, Effective from the First of Next Month 131

China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Hankou route is now scheduled to increase one flight from the first of next month, and at the same time, the flight schedule will be advanced. The departure time of the Shanghai-Beiping route will also be changed, effective June 1. The details are as follows:

Increased Flights 132

The company's Shanghai-Hankou route was originally scheduled for flights between Shanghai and Hankou every day from Tuesday to Sunday at 8:00 am, arriving at around 3:00 pm respectively. Now, due to the extraordinary development of the route's business, passengers and mail are quite crowded. In order to facilitate travel, the company has decided to fly as usual on Mondays, which were originally rest days, adding one flight to meet the needs. That is, there will be flights every day of the week, and the company has decided to implement this from next month (June) 1st.

Earlier Flights 133

In addition, the company, considering that it is now summer and the weather is getting hotter, will also advance the flight time. All westbound and eastbound flights between Shanghai and Hankou will take off at 7:00 am every day, arriving at 2:05 pm respectively. At the same time, the flight time of the Shanghai-Beiping route will also be advanced. That is, every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday at 6:30 am, flights will depart south from Beiping, and on Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday at 6:00 am, flights will depart north from Shanghai, all arriving at 3:30 pm in the afternoon.

Notice to All Stations 134

After deciding on the above-mentioned new regulations, the company specially notified all stations to inform them. The original text reads: "It is hereby notified that from June 1st, the departure times of the company's Shanghai-Hankou and Shanghai-Beiping routes will be advanced (times as above). From the same day, the Shanghai-Hankou route will also be changed to daily flights, with flights also on Mondays. Accordingly, this letter is sent to you in the hope that you will check and inform. The advertisements at your station should be corrected the day before and the style should be cut and sent back for verification. The new timetable will be sent separately after it is printed."

Rent Reduction Committee Held Joint Meeting Yesterday, Scheduled to Summon Representatives from District Branches for Discussion 135

The Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee held its eighth joint meeting of the Executive Design Law Committee at 4:00 pm yesterday. More than 20 people attended, including Zhang Yichen, Zhou Fuzhang, Zhang Xianfang, Wang Hesong, Cai Qiajun, Wang Honghui, Li Ruzhang, Chen Binghui, Jiang Chiping, Chen Jiufeng, Yu Hualong, Li Ao Kui, Zhang Juansheng, Shu Huizhen, Hu Yibo, Hong Songjiong, and Wang Xiangu. Matters for discussion: (1) The case of submitting a report to the council on the reasons for rent reduction and refuting the Shanghai Real Estate Association's letter to the Municipal Council was resolved to be handled by the Secretariat as soon as possible. (3) The case of hiring legal counsel according to the previous resolution was resolved to appoint the lawyers present at the meeting today as legal counsel. (4) The case of requesting the court not to abuse provisional attachments was resolved, with Zhang Yichen, Zhou Fuzhang, Chen Jiufeng, and others going to the First Special District, the Second Special District, and the District Court to petition. (5) The case of the Dadji Road Sanduoli Branch's letter requesting the committee to entrust a lawyer was resolved to recommend lawyer Wang Xiangu to handle it and reply to the branch to appoint its own lawyer. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

The Rent Reduction Promotion Association Contributes Opinions on Rent Reduction: The Relationship between Rent Reduction and Prosperity is Close, Specially Sent to the Council for Reference 136

The Rent Reduction Promotion Association of various groups in this city held a standing committee meeting at 2:00 pm yesterday and sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council, contributing opinions on rent reduction for reference. The details are as follows:

Standing Committee Meeting 137

The Rent Reduction Promotion Association of various groups in this city held a standing committee meeting at the association's office at 2:00 pm yesterday. Nine people attended, including Song Tiren, Yang Xiongchan, Zhang Gang, Jin Chuxiang, Huang Zhensheng, Zhu Shujian, Qiu Liangyu, Hong Songjiong, and Wang Tingsheng. The meeting was chaired by Qiu Liangyu, and the following cases were discussed: (A) The case of whether to notify all industries to deposit the rent in the bank after stopping payment from June was resolved to be submitted to the executive committee meeting. (B) The case of sending a letter to the council requesting a copy of the Real Estate Association's opinion letter to be sent to the association for research was resolved and passed. (C) The case of nominating Chen Yongnian as the director of the organization department was resolved to be submitted to the executive committee for election to comply with the election policy. The meeting adjourned at 4:30 pm.

Contribution of Opinions 138

The association specially sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council yesterday, contributing opinions on rent reduction. The original text reads: "The Shanghai rent reduction movement has lasted for four months and has become a prerequisite for Shanghai's prosperity, which is attracting the attention of Chinese and foreign people. Recently, we learned that your council has been instructed by the municipal government to discuss the issue of rent. Therefore, we would like to offer our humble opinions as follows: (1) We believe that housing is one of the four major elements of life and an indispensable thing for mankind. The prices of clothing and food are now much lower than before. The reason for this is related to the social economy, that is, the prices of clothing and food change with the social economy. The same is true for rent. What was the price of rent before the rise of trust transactions? Anyone who has been in Shanghai for a long time can tell. In the past ten years or so, whether it is a resident or a shop, although it seems to bear this high rent with reluctance and pain on the surface, the desire for rent reduction has been eager to try. Therefore, the current widespread rent reduction movement can respond to every call with swift momentum, which shows that it is entirely due to accumulation and indignation, which is the natural principle among human beings. Since the outbreak of the two major changes of "September 18" and "January 28", the social economy has felt extremely uneasy, and Shanghai's prosperity will be declared bankrupt. The so-called big price cuts in the current commercial market are everywhere. Other examples include the recall of agricultural plates, unemployment of workers, and the increasing number of rent arrears cases in the courts. Based on this, it is enough to prove that the reduction or non-reduction of rent is closely related to Shanghai's prosperity. This is one thing that should be noted. (2) We have heard that the silver and money industries are deeply concerned about the issue of rent reduction. The reason they hold is that rent is the interest on real estate. If the rent is reduced, it will inevitably affect its property price. Because many houses in Shanghai are mortgaged to the silver and money industries, the trend of rent reduction must not be allowed to grow. However, it is too rigid to know this. It should be known that the silver and money industries also make mortgages on silk, rice, yarn, etc. Judging from past facts, the price has fallen miserably after being mortgaged, which is often heard. The mortgage of real estate is the same. Why worry? The current rent reduction has been forced by circumstances. For example, in the distant past, countries such as Germany and Japan also had government orders for rent reduction. Recently, in our country, Nanjing's rent reduction and the Central Political Council's promulgation of rent standards, our association dares to say that the rent reduction movement is actually beneficial to society. All industries are members of society. If it is beneficial to society, then there is no harm to the industry that does mortgages. May I ask if the increase in land prices in Shanghai is not caused by ordinary tenants? Because tenants gather together in that area, each running their lives, becoming a market, resulting in the daily increase in land prices, the so-called sacrifice of the public, creating their personal wealth, this has been explained in detail in the third lecture of the Principle of People's Livelihood. This is the second thing that should be noted. (3) There are many disputes about rent reduction methods. Some advocate the main area principle, some advocate the interest principle, and some advocate the house price principle. However, Shanghai has a vast area and houses are densely packed. If the above-mentioned principles are followed, it is necessary to start an investigation, but often those who do not understand the overall situation will conceal the facts. It is feared that it will not be easy to do so even in a few years. It is to save society and disturb society. It is often seen that the methods formulated by the Rent Reduction Committee are calculated by the year of construction, which is suitable for the urgent needs of society. This rent reduction movement is an unavoidable move, aimed at promoting the market, helping each other, uniting, and saving the crisis together, and there is no hostility between them. This rent reduction method should be submitted to your council for adoption by the municipal government, and the formulated methods should be implemented immediately. This is the third thing that should be noted. In summary, it seems to be practical and easy to implement. We hope that you will examine it carefully."

Stalemate on Both Sides 140

More than 5,000 workers and Chinese staff of the New Factory of British American Tobacco Company, in order to support the workers of the Old Factory, announced a general strike on the 24th, resulting in a complete standstill of work in various departments. Even the cigarettes in stock cannot be shipped. Yesterday, the workers of the factory continued to strike. The British-American small steamer drivers also joined the strike yesterday after the trade union sent a letter of warning. The company re-hired White Russian drivers.

Inside the factory, such as in the engine room and the furnace room, there are still a small number of White Russians working, but all other work has stopped. The company has not made any statement so far, and the workers have not sent anyone to negotiate with the company. The two sides are still in a stalemate.

The Shanghai Municipal Government believes that the situation of the British-American workers' strike is serious. If a solution is not found quickly, it will not only affect the workers' livelihood but also affect local security. The representatives also requested the Municipal Government to order the factory to resume operations immediately in order to quell the strike. The Ministry of Finance Approved the Chamber of Commerce to Reduce the Export Tax on Peanuts for Three Months, Reducing 60% of the Original Tax Rate 148

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Miscellaneous Grain, Oil Cake, and Allied Trades Association, requesting that, following the example of Qingdao, the Ministry of Finance be requested to reduce the export tax on peanuts and other local products shipped overseas from Shanghai and exempt the transit tax for transportation to various ports in the country for two years, etc. The Chamber immediately reported the situation to the Ministry of Finance. The original text has been seen in previous reports. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance approved the Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating, "Received and noted. After verification by the Ministry, it has been approved to reduce the originally set export tax rate for peanuts, peanut kernels, and peanut oil shipped overseas from Shanghai by 60%, limited to those shipped overseas within three months, that is, from May 26 of this year to August 25. The Director-General of Customs has also been ordered to inform the customs to comply. As for the request to exempt the transit tax, the Ministry has carefully examined and verified that peanuts and other products are major local products of Shandong, which have a direct relationship with the market in Qingdao. The situation is different from those transshipped to Shanghai, and Shanghai is a gathering area for various freights. The amount of peanuts transshipped has no significant impact on the prosperity or decline of the market and cannot be compared with Qingdao, which mainly trades in peanuts. The request cannot be approved. You should immediately inform them accordingly. This approval."

Report of the Red Swastika Society on the Handling of Disaster Relief Work in Pingyin and Dong'a Counties: 2,500 Hectares of Fertile Land Have Been Dredged, but Two-Thirds Still Lack Funds for Further Work 152

The Shanghai General Office of the World Red Swastika Society, in response to the severe flooding in Dongping and Dong'a counties in Shandong Province last year, specifically raised disaster relief funds and handed them over to the Jinan Red Swastika Society to carry out emergency relief efforts. This included dredging the Yellow River estuary in Dong'a County and areas south to Songjiatun in Dongping County. To date, 7,600 yuan has been raised, along with donations from the Provincial Disaster Relief Association and the Northeast Charity Federation, totaling 25,600 yuan. We have now received a report from the project office regarding the dredging situation, stating that the Society's handling of the emergency relief and work relief in Pingyin and Dong'a counties was supported by philanthropists from various provinces, the Provincial Disaster Relief Association, and others. A large-scale porridge kitchen was set up in the disaster area, and a work relief office was organized to begin dredging the entire section of the Yellow River estuary. The project extends from the Yellow River estuary in Dong'a County in the north to Songjiatun in Dongping County in the south, a total of forty *li* (approximately 20 kilometers). The northern section, where sedimentation is highest and work is most difficult, accounts for one-third of the entire section. This construction first started here, and a total of 4,800 to 6,000 local laborers were gathered, each receiving 1.3 *jiao* for food per day. Foremen were appointed from village chiefs, numbering 357, each receiving 2.3 *jiao* for food per day. It was originally planned that this dangerous section could be completed in twenty days. However, due to rain twice and snow once, work was delayed. Furthermore, the passage of bandit gangs under the leadership of Liu further slowed the work, extending it to thirty-two days before this dangerous section was completed. A total of 20,421.5 yuan was spent. Villages contributed grain worth over 20,000 yuan, bringing the total cost to over 40,000 yuan. Only one-third of the entire project was completed, which is a significant discrepancy from the original estimate. According to last winter's original estimate by the Dongping County government, the entire project of forty *li* would only require 20,000 yuan. Only after actual construction began was it realized that the original estimate was far too low. The County government was only aware of the work within Dongping County, which was not very difficult, and was unaware that the area within Dong'a County had been heavily silted up by the Yellow River last autumn, as high as mounds. Currently, there is a constant stream of appeals for outside funds, and the villagers are also struggling to provide grain. Furthermore, the planting season has arrived, so work had to be suspended and the water released. An estimated 2,500 *qing* (approximately 16,667 hectares) of land has been drained, all of which is planted with barley, with some sorghum. This success is due to the generosity and advocacy of major philanthropists. However, in the Pingyin and Dong'a areas, over 5,000 *qing* of land have been flooded. This dredging project has only covered one-third, and only half of the flooded land has been drained. If the remaining two-thirds of the southern section can be dredged, all 5,000 *qing* of land can be drained. This is a fundamental aspect of disaster relief that cannot be delayed. According to the contractor's report, the southern section is easier than the northern section, and another 25,000 yuan would ensure its completion. Therefore, repeated requests have been made to the Shandong Provincial Government in recent months, but only 5,000 yuan has been approved for continued funding, leaving a significant shortfall and risking the failure of the entire effort. It is urgently hoped that the great philanthropists in Shanghai will continue to provide assistance so that the entire project can be completed and all 5,000 *qing* of flooded land can be drained. Not only will the people be spared starvation and be able to cultivate their land like those in other counties, but the philanthropists will also have cultivated a field of merit without end. Furthermore, Qinghemen is silted up every year due to backflow of Yellow River water. If the entire project is completed, it can guarantee a small wheat harvest within two or three years. However, annual dredging would be difficult. The heads of all townships and towns in the disaster area have jointly decided to build a mud dredging boat. If there is accumulated silt, the boat can be used to冲挖(*chungwa* to use the force of water from a boat to break up the mud and silt). This would require less effort and achieve greater results. In this way, the generosity of the philanthropists will never be wasted. The cost of building the boat is around 80,000 yuan, which will be funded from the harvest of the drained land. This is stated jointly.

Import Tax Evasion on Foreign Sugar Smuggled from Dalian; Unloaded at Chuanjiacun and Xinggepu; Then Transferred to Junks to be Smuggled into the Interior 159

Since the import tax on foreign sugar was increased, the amount of foreign sugar smuggled into our country for sale in the past year has accounted for as much as four-tenths of the total amount. Not only has customs revenue suffered a major loss, but the impact on sugar merchants' businesses has been even greater. In order to strictly investigate the source of sugar smuggling, the Tianjin Customs specially dispatched agents to various ports along the coast of North China to secretly investigate. After months of investigation, they discovered that the smuggling originated from Chuanjiacun, Xinggepu and other places near Dalian, where foreign sugar was secretly loaded onto ships, then transferred to junks along the coast and privately transported to Qingdao, Haizhou, and outside Wusongkou, and then smuggled into the interior. In this year, the amount smuggled into our country has reached several million yuan. It is reported that the Japanese authorities in Dalian have been notified to strictly cooperate in the investigation and crackdown.

Assassination of Wang Delong, Captain of the Nanhui Detective Team, Sentenced to Death 160

Zhu Zifan, captain of the detective team of the Nanhui County Public Security Bureau, was shot and killed at 8:20 PM on the 11th of this month at the Huibin Hotel, No. 13, Lane 369, Guangdong Road, by Wang Delong (also known as Jinshan) and Chen Delong (also known as Jinshan), both from Pudong. The main text of the verdict is: Wang Delong is sentenced to death for premeditated murder. The handgun and six bullets are confiscated.

Intense Gunfire Like Interlocking Beads; Bandits in Zhabei Fought Fiercely to Resist Arrest; Shopkeeper Peeks Through Glass Door to See the Situation; Tenant's Wife Urgently Reports to Police for Arrest; | One Bandit Killed, Three Bandits Captured Alive | 161

The *shikumen* (stone gate) residence at No. 15 Taixingfang, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, houses Hu Peigeng, a secret 波(*bo* person, a transliteration indicating a foreigner) from the Shunchang Machine Factory on Baotong Road, and Bao Wanglin, a postal worker. The attic is occupied by artist Shi Ruihua's family. Hu is the sub-landlord. The factory specializes in manufacturing various flashlights. Since the boycott of foreign goods and the promotion of domestic goods, business has greatly flourished, resulting in a slight surplus, which was coveted by bandits. Yesterday morning at 7:30 AM, Hu's female servant Jiang Dongshi was washing a chamber pot at the back door when four bandits wearing long gowns and short shirts suddenly broke in through the

Back Door 162

and forced the female servant inside, brandishing handguns, forbidding her to make a sound. They drove the Hu family and others into a dark room behind the living room and held them captive. Then they ransacked the boxes and chests, looting Hu Peigeng's jade ring, gemstone ring, pearl necklace, etc., Shi Ruihua's gold ring and woolen coat, etc., and Bao Wanglin's leather suitcase containing $16 in paper money and $0.11 in small coins. Just as they were about to escape with the stolen goods, the bandits did not notice Bao Wanglin's wife, who was outside Hu's back door buying broad beans from a vendor when they entered the house. The vendor through the glass door

Saw the Bandits Entering 163

and quickly reported the robbery to the police at Post No. 44 in the Fifth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who relayed it to District Chief Liang Fuchu. Liang Fuchu led Superintendent Wang Molin, Officer Gao Chunshan, the entire patrol squad, and detectives Yu Hanwen and Lu Hexiang, fully armed, to the address. Seeing that the front and back doors of the house were locked, District Chief Liang urgently ordered the police and detectives to surround the house and ordered the other residents to stay inside. At the same time, he directed Police Chief Wang Molin and others to cross the wall from the roof of No. 10 and climb to the drying platform of No. 15. The police and detectives obeyed orders and rushed forward bravely. The bandits heard the urgent knocking on the door below and realized that something was wrong. They quickly turned around and ran upstairs, but the police chiefs who had crossed the wall from the roof of No. 10 had already reached the drying platform of No. 15. Seeing that the front and back exits were blocked, the bandits opened fire in desperation. The police and detectives also returned fire. The gunfire on both sides was as dense as interlocking beads, as if

Facing a Major Enemy 164

As a result, the bandits were overwhelmed. At the same time, the police and detectives successively rushed in and apprehended three bandits upstairs. They then saw another bandit resisting arrest below the stairs. They quickly aimed at his chest and fired a shot, hitting him. He fell to the ground on the spot and died, bleeding profusely. His death was horrifying. They seized a "No. 29157" six-inch Harmon gun, a cartridge case, and two remaining bullets. They were then brought to the District for interrogation. The bandits confessed, saying, "Lu Erbao, 26 years old, from Taicang," and directly admitted to the robbery. When interrogated about the other two bandits, they confessed, "Sun Quanjing, 25 years old, from Shandong, lives in Room 38 of the Tianran Hotel in the concession. The

Dead Accomplice 165

is Li Er, in his twenties, from Taicang. There are also accomplices on the run, Little Brother and Lin Amao." They also revealed their hiding places. Yu Bingsheng (also known as Amao), 25 years old, from Shaoxing, also admitted that he was led to Hu's house by Wang Xingmiao, who was still at large, to commit robbery. The officials then led the bandits, together with Chinese and Western detectives from the French Concession Police Station, to No. 210 Caishi Road to arrest Wang and to No. 170 Mingdelili, Malong Road, to arrest Lin, but they had already fled upon hearing the news and disappeared without a trace. They were then taken to the District for detention. The seized stolen goods were identified by the victims. The three bandits and the handgun were handed over to the General Bureau for legal proceedings. The police and detectives bravely captured the bandits and did not let any escape, which is commendable. as a reward.

The Continental Daily Praises Xinhua Village: Elegant and Quiet Environment, Excellent Facilities 166

According to the Continental Daily on May 24, "The population and houses of Shanghai are increasing day by day. It has become the most serious problem today for new and old residents who want to find spacious housing and a quiet environment because of the weakness of social and economic forces. Some people live in the bustling areas of the concession, and because of the high rent, living in a pigeonhole has become a popular saying. The houses are small, the air is full of smoke and dust, and it is constantly noisy. Some people move to the western suburbs of Shanghai because it is more suitable for living conditions, but they suffer from the high cost. Therefore, the former live in apartments and climb mountains to get home, while the latter travel too far and are covered in dust. The Xinhua Bank pays close attention to the housing problem in Shanghai and attempts to solve the housing problem for the general public with their enthusiasm for serving society. Therefore, Xinhua Village was built on Xitiyuhui Road in northern Shanghai, with convenient location, convenient transportation, excellent environment, and economical living conditions. Xinhua Village covers an area of 50 *mu* (approximately 3.3 hectares) and is only one mile from Hongkou Park. There are main roads to the Public Concession and the Shanghai Haixin District. The house foundations in the new village have been demarcated. Trees are planted between the houses, and there are clean and elegant lawns and gardens. Exquisite and beautiful houses are being built. When the entire project is completed in the future, it will definitely become the best and newest residential area in Shanghai. The method of purchasing housing in Xinhua Village is different from that of general real estate companies. The Xinhua Bank knows that the general public lacks the whole amount of money to purchase a house, so it adopts the method of paying in installments, combining repayment with rent payment. It can be very easily and unconsciously, after a few years, the house will belong to you. The village is surrounded by beautiful and quiet countryside, without any of the hustle and bustle of the city, but with wide and flat roads and convenient transportation. If you take a private car, it only takes 13 minutes. Public buses also only take 22 minutes to travel between the new village and the Bund. In addition, there is a route that is Tiantong'an and Jiangwan, which is where the Songhu Railway passes. Therefore, it is also very convenient for general businessmen and women to live there. Although Xinhua Village is not in the concession area, the various facilities are as convenient as those in the concession. For example, water and electricity are supplied by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, and telephone calls can be directly connected to the Public Concession and the French Concession. Water and electricity fees and rent are also cheaper than in the concession. In addition, the village is very close to the school district, and there are all levels of schools from kindergartens to universities, such as Shanghai Law School, Chizhi College, Fudan University, Aiguo Women's School, and Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School. In the future, for the convenience of the residents, small vegetable markets and mailboxes will also be set up. In addition to the above-mentioned advantages, Xinhua Village also has a very good outdoor sports environment. Usually, you can take a walk in Hongkou Park, or swim in the park's swimming pool, or go horseback riding on the open road in Jiangwan. It is indeed an ideal paradise."

The Liu Shufan et al. Case Concludes; Prosecutor's Argument Divided into Two Parts; Debate Concluded Yesterday, Sentencing Scheduled 167

The case of Liu Shufan, former Director of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, and others, for embezzlement and harming the national treasury, was prosecuted by the Prosecutor's Office of the First Special District Court. Judge Liu Yugui repeatedly held court hearings. The details have been repeatedly recorded in the newspapers. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu, together with Prosecutor Zhong Qing, continued to hear the case. Liang Banxing, secretary of the preparatory office of the Daxin Company, was summoned to court to investigate the situation of the defendant Zhao Baoshan using a portion of the commission from the land purchase by the Savings and Remittance Bureau to subscribe for Daxin shares. According to Liang, the company received 23,025 taels of silver from four households, Yang Wubentang, Yang Shude, Zhao Huiji, etc., equivalent to 30,000 Hong Kong dollars, which was delivered by the Zhao surname. He also presented the receipt books and subscription forms. Judge Liu then asked Zhao Baoshan and Yang Peichang about the commissions they received and how Zhao purchased Daxin shares. Then, he presented the postal savings regulations and repeatedly cross-examined Liu Shufan and others about the procedures for withdrawing savings with checks. Then, he ordered the debate to begin. Prosecutor Zhong first stated the arguments of the case, roughly dividing the case into two parts: (1) The part involving the commission of Zhao Baoshan and Yang Peichang; (2) The part involving the purchase and sale of government bonds by Liu Shufan and others. Zhong then stated the reasons for the defendants' crimes in the government bond trading incident, saying that the usual practice is for banks to require customers to deposit margin before buying and selling government bonds on behalf of customers. However, the defendants advanced over 400,000 yuan to the Daison Company for buying and selling government bonds without calculating interest, while the 100,000 taels of silver deposited in the account of Liu Jianhou, which they claimed to be margin, was calculated daily. This clearly favored one party over the other. In fact, the name of the Daison Company account was actually the defendant himself, and he deliberately created a name to cover up the facts. Their actions have violated Articles 136, 140, and 366 of the Criminal Code. Next, he stated the reasons for the crimes of Zhao Baoshan and others obtaining illegal commissions, saying that the amount obtained by the defendants in the two land purchases was 135,000 taels and 29,000 taels, respectively, of which Yang Jianping shared 34,325 taels. According to the customary practice of land sales, the commission is generally 1% or 1.5% of the property price. However, the property price on Albert Road was 1.2 million taels, and the commission reached 150,000 taels, which is 1/8 of the property price. There has never been such a shocking commission. It is clear that the defendants colluded with Yang Jianping, internally and externally, to inflate the property price and openly embezzle the funds. The facts are clear, and he requested that the defendants be judged according to law. Then, the defense lawyers of the defendants, Liu Chongyou, Shi Jiong, Cao Shoulin, Zou Yu, and Liu Shifang, defended their clients in turn. The court then adjourned to schedule sentencing.

An Old Servant of the Sheng Xingcun Family Embezzles Valuables After Twenty Years of Service; Addicted to Habits, Short on Funds, Stealing Important Clothes Worth Thousands 168

Sheng Xingcun, formerly a Palace Guardian of the Qing Dynasty, has a residence located at 526 Jing'an Temple Road, a large and spacious property. However, due to the building's age and dilapidated walls, the rear of the house is being renovated. As a result, all the important trunks and belongings of his descendants' various households are stored in one room, called the storage room, and sealed. A servant named Ruan Ronggen is assigned to guard it. Ruan, a native of Anhui, was hired by Sheng Gongbao's second concubine and has served for twenty years. He is usually very honest and has no bad habits. However, recently, due to indulging in certain habits, he has been short on funds. After much deliberation, he takes a risk. On the 22nd of this month, at 2:30 AM, before dawn, in the quiet of the night, he colludes with a relative, someone named Jia, to open the locked storage room. They select two boxes of important clothes, valued at 9,554 yuan, and steal them. They hire rickshaws to take them to a friend's house, intending to pawn them later. The matter is discovered by the Sheng family. Noticing that the seals on the boxes are broken, they inspect further and realize that clothes worth ten thousand yuan are missing. However, they don't know who stole them at the time, and Ruan remains calm and continues to serve as usual. Subsequently, Huang Dazhong, representing the Sheng family, reports the matter to the New Gate Police Station. The station immediately dispatches Chinese Detective Tang Jian, Yao Yuanlong, Detective Lu Gendi, Jiang Juwu, Constable Xia Yeshan, and Western Detective Qi Jiasheng. After days of detailed investigation, they find the Sheng family's servant, Ruan Ronggen, suspicious and evasive. Yesterday, they take Ruan to the police station for questioning. Ruan confesses to the theft and leads the Chinese and Western detectives to 334 Mei Baek Road and 97 Father Jin Road in the French Concession. There, they apprehend two more suspects, Dou Guanghua and Yin Bengen, and recover most of the stolen goods, over 7,700 yuan worth of clothes. They are all taken to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, they are sent to the First Special Court, Criminal Division Eight. The police station's lawyer, Gan Jingguang, presents the case and requests a postponement to investigate the remaining stolen goods. Judge Wu Zehan briefly questions the defendants and orders them to be remanded in custody separately, pending further investigation and questioning.

### Swearing by Execution, Shen Mingming Claims Framing by Detective Xu Guirong, But Convicted and Sentenced to Two Years Imprisonment Due to Evidence 169

Shen Mingming, a local resident of Ninghe Road, Yangshupu, with no house number, is an elderly man of seventy years. He is a local bailiff with a prosperous family. Recently, Chinese Detective Xu Guirong of the Narcotics Division discovers that he is selling "red pills" (narcotics). He reports this to Western Detective Chief Bai Pu, who, on the morning of the previous day at around 10 AM, secretly goes with a court warrant. They arrest Shen at his address and find a "double corner" coin, used as a marker by an informant who bought pills from him, in his possession. They also find four packages of "red pills," estimated to be several thousand, in an old bamboo basket of clothes under the porch, and an opium lamp in the bedroom. Nothing else is found. They are all taken to the Yangshupu Police Station. The head of the station orders him detained. The next morning, he is sent to the First Special District Court, Criminal Division Three. The Municipal Council lawyer, Wang Yuetang, states that on the 16th and 17th of this month, Detective Xu sent an informant to the defendant's place, each time buying two small packets of pills for two "corners." The third time, he used a penknife to mark the "double corner" coin as a secret sign. He then bought another small packet, and the Chinese and Western detectives immediately entered and arrested him. He is now being prosecuted under Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law. He presents the confiscated evidence: the "double corner" coin, seven packages of "red pills" of various sizes, and the opium lamp for inspection. Subsequently, according to the Chinese and Western detectives' report of the investigation, the defendant claims that he does not sell "red pills," that he has known Detective Xu for many years, and that there is a feud between them, so he is deliberately framing him. He says that yesterday morning, Xu sent his colleagues to invite him out for tea twice, but he refused. During that time, they secretly put the "red pills" in the bamboo basket, and the "double corner" coin was also put into his pocket when he was arrested. He states that the opium lamp was used when he was sick. He says that if he were selling "red pills," he would gladly accept execution. Detective Xu denies the defendant's claims. A woman from Suzhou, Wu Sijin, testifies that she is the defendant's tenant and has lived with him for over ten years, and that he does not sell "red pills." An informant from Haizhou named Zhang Defa testifies that he bought a small packet of "red pills" for two "corners" from the defendant three times, and that he personally handed them over each time. Judge Xiao Xiefen, based on the conclusive evidence, sentences Shen Mingming to two years imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 yuan. The evidence is confiscated. The defendant's lawyer declares an appeal and requests bail, presenting a guarantee from dozens of neighboring shops, which is rejected. He is returned to custody.

The Two Road Bureaus Collect a Joint Transport Car and Sedan Chair Surcharge for Moganshan; Agreed Method Extended for One Year 172

The joint collection method of transport car and sedan chair surcharge for Moganshan, previously agreed upon by the Two Road Bureaus, the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau, and the Moganshan Management Office, roughly stipulates that the Highway Bureau and the Two Road Bureaus collect a surcharge for joint transport passengers' cars and sedan chairs on behalf of the Moganshan Management Bureau. The surcharge rates are: (A) Car surcharge: First, second, and third class passengers, adults 20 cents per person, children (age according to railway regulations) 10 cents per person; (B) Sedan chair surcharge: sedan chair bearers 10 cents per person. Those who purchase round-trip tickets will be charged double the above rates. The effective period of this method was originally until the end of the 22nd year. The bureau intends to continue for another year after the expiration, and has separately sent letters to the Road Bureau to agree. The bureau believes that this agreement is beneficial to the overall construction of the mountain, so it should do its best to support it. However, the wording in Article 5 of the agreement, "The Railway Bureau is represented by the Chief of the Hangzhou Train Section," should be changed to "The Railway Bureau is represented by the Chief of the Hangzhou-Jiaza Train Section or the Manager of the Moganshan Railway Hotel" to conform to the current organization of the road. Railway staff traveling from Hangzhou to Moganshan or from the mountain back to Hangzhou will provide proof by a letter from the Section Chief or Hotel Manager to avoid paying the car and sedan chair surcharge. It has been separately replied and ordered the relevant departments to comply.

Tuberculosis Prevention Work in the Hygiene Campaign; The Chinese Anti-Tuberculosis Association Formulates Guidelines 175

The 13th Municipal Hygiene Campaign will begin on the 19th of next month. The tuberculosis prevention work will be carried out by the Chinese Anti-Tuberculosis Association. It is learned that the Anti-Tuberculosis Association has finalized the following guidelines for tuberculosis prevention work during the Hygiene Campaign:

Publicity Aspects: In order to raise public awareness of tuberculosis prevention, the association will organize a costumed publicity team to participate in performances in public places. It will also hold large-scale tuberculosis prevention lectures in the eastern, southern, western, and northern districts of the city. Workers and their families are welcome to attend to gain common knowledge of tuberculosis prevention. It is also planned to open all parks in the city and have the association post various illustrated slogans and other publicity materials in the parks to achieve widespread publicity.

Practical Work: In addition to publicity, the association plans to carry out temporary services during the campaign period. The association will designate four elementary schools in the eastern, western, southern, and northern districts of the city to conduct tuberculosis tests. It will also contact famous hospitals in the city to provide free tuberculosis examinations for citizens during the campaign. X-rays will be charged at half price. Doctors registered with the Municipal Health Bureau will also charge half price for tuberculosis examinations for citizens during this campaign period.

Xie Shanshu Commits Suicide by Poison; Swallowing Opium in a Hongkou Apartment; Letter Addressed to Chen Rutian; Notes on the Back of a Photo of Women Together 180

At around noon the day before yesterday, a middle-aged man of about thirty years of age, speaking Cantonese, wearing a blue-grey silk spring gown and a grey felt hat, checked into Room No. 2 of the Jinde Apartment at 737 North Sichuan Road. He looked haggard and walked unsteadily. He claimed to be named Li Dechen, a merchant from Guangdong, 29 years old. He paid a room fee of two yuan. After the tea boy brought the tea and water and left, he closed the door tightly. At 5 PM, he opened the door and called the tea boy to buy him food. Around 7 PM, he ordered a bowl of noodles from the tea boy, ate it, and then went to bed. Unexpectedly, at around midnight, there was a groan in the room. The tea boys heard it and suspected something was wrong. They rushed forward and knocked on the door, but there was no response for a long time. They quickly reported to the accounting room and tried to use a wooden ladder to look into the room from the air vent with a flashlight. They saw the guest lying stiffly in bed, motionless. Knowing that something had happened, they climbed in from the balcony and turned on the light. They saw him foaming at the mouth and barely breathing. They immediately reported to the 1st Precinct of the 5th District and notified the Fire Brigade to send a fire truck to take him to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. However, he had taken too much poison and died at around 4 AM yesterday morning. The police station sent officers to investigate and reported to the court for an inspection yesterday morning. At the same time, they found two suicide notes under the pillow. One was addressed to the apartment, asking them to notify his friend Chen Rutian to handle the funeral. The other was addressed to Chen Rutian, stating, "Last night, after eating at Tan Manji, I went to the Hongkou Hotel to commit suicide by poisoning. Because I bought too little opium (six jiao), I suffered all night without dying. Today I took poison, buying one yuan's worth of opium, which should kill me," signed "Brother Xie Xiushan." Therefore, it was learned that the deceased's real name was Xie Xiushan. He had first attempted suicide by poisoning at the Hongkou Hotel, but had failed. So he moved to the Hongkou Apartment to end his life. The reason for the suicide is unknown. A photograph of the deceased and some women was found next to the deceased's body. On the back was written, "Please have Chen Rutian publish this photo in the newspaper to ask someone to claim the body," The 1st Precinct of the 5th District is currently investigating Chen Rutian, hoping to uncover the truth.

Domestic Electrical Machinery is Being Promoted 183

Most of the machinery used by power plants across the country are imported products. The money flowing out of the electricity industry every year is enormous. It is recently learned that the New Electricity World magazine, hosted by Mr. Deng Zi'an, has an electrical industry introduction department that specializes in promoting domestically produced electrical machinery. The magazine has been in Shanghai for more than two years and has connections with power plants and electrical experts across the country. Currently, the introduction department is promoting domestically produced electrical transformers manufactured by Yizhong Fuji Machinery and Porcelain Electric Company. Mr. Deng has issued a letter to power plants and electrical experts across the country, inviting them to work together to use domestic products. It is hoped that this can also be a good opportunity for Chinese manufacturers of electrical machinery. The letter states: "Dear Sir, Today, if China wants to become wealthy and strong, it must increase domestic production. Our country's electricity industry is growing rapidly, and the electrical machinery it needs is mostly purchased from abroad. The annual amount of money exported has reached more than ten million yuan. The industry should find ways to prevent this outflow. Recently, the whole country is promoting domestic products. If everyone adopts a portion of domestic goods and focuses on manufacturing, the domestic industry will be revitalized to a certain extent, and the country will preserve a portion of its vitality. As for transformers needed in the electrical industry, Shanghai's Yizhong Fuji Machinery and Porcelain Electric Company manufactures them, specializing in transformers, current limiting tables, and various electrical porcelain materials. The company has been established for nearly fifteen years, and most of the managers are technical experts. All the power plants that have used their products have praised them, and the prices are lower than imported products. Domestically produced electrical machinery has already replaced foreign products. We hope that domestic electrical factories will promote and use these transformers as much as possible to show the glory of domestic products, increase the country's wealth, and encourage manufacturers to make further efforts. We believe that you are enthusiastic about the domestic electricity industry and will not be left behind. We hope that you can work together to achieve the joy of self-sufficiency as soon as possible. If your factory wants to try these transformers, you can directly contact the company (110 Hankou Road, Shanghai) for detailed inquiries. If you have any inconveniences in communicating and inquiring directly, our introduction department can handle everything for you. Out of the sincerity of promoting domestic products, we are sending this letter to you. Deng Zi'an of the Introduction Department of Shanghai New Electricity World Magazine."

The Municipal Gazetteer Hall Publishes a Collection of Periodicals 184

The Shanghai Municipal Gazetteer Hall is working hard to compile the city's gazetteer with the spirit of unity and hard work. In order to solicit scholars' guidance and public criticism, it has printed several drafts in quarterly installments and published a periodical, which is distributed to various sectors. Not only is the status of the hall's work specifically proved by the periodical, but also its hard work and uncompromising attitude are spread to the academic community. In a very short period of time, people have not only been able to predict that the Shanghai Municipal Gazetteer will open a new era in Chinese local gazetteers, but also confirmed the hall as one of China's important academic institutions. However, due to funding constraints, the number of copies of the periodical published by the hall is very limited. Before it could be widely distributed, it was already requested. Many groups and individuals in the city and other places have sent letters requesting copies because they have not been able to read it, which the hall deeply regrets. It is learned that the hall is taking advantage of the full year of publication of this periodical to carefully proofread and reprint 300 copies of the year's periodicals, which are bound together to meet the needs. The bound volume has more than 1,100 pages and about 700,000 words. It contains historical records of various sectors of Shanghai, including politics, the Public Concession, the French Concession, diplomacy, finance, art, industry, and social undertakings, ranging from tens of thousands to more than 100,000 words. It is essential for those who are interested in studying Shanghai and want to understand the important history of China in the past century. Each volume is priced at five yuan, plus one yuan for postage outside the city. Those who need it can purchase it directly from the hall at 291 Sapo Sai Road, Shanghai, to avoid missing the opportunity again.

Car Driver Appeals for Reduced Sentence in Manslaughter Case 188

Car driver Gao Chunsheng, at approximately 9:00 AM on March 22nd of this year, drove private car number 892, owned by Russian doctor Mai Qi (transliteration), eastward along Avenue Joffre in the French Concession to the tram station near Rue Lupan. Due to the driver's carelessness, Wang Mo (courtesy name Bingqing) from Shaoxing, who was the head of the documentation section of the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance, was hit and killed. The French police's traffic department arrested Gao and transferred him to the Second Special District Local Court for public prosecution. The victim's family also filed a civil suit, seeking damages of 30,000 yuan. The first instance sentenced Gao to three years in prison and ordered him to compensate the victim's family with 5,000 yuan in damages. Gao, dissatisfied with the original judgment, appealed to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The court recently held a hearing. In the private suit portion, an out-of-court settlement was reached with compensation of 2,600 yuan, to be paid in three installments. The public suit portion was declared closed, pending sentencing. The previous report had already noted these details. Yesterday, Judge Guo, along with Assessors Sun and Fan, held a hearing and announced the judgment: the original judgment was overturned, and Gao Chunsheng was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for causing death due to negligence in his profession. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be deducted from the sentence at a rate of two days for one day, reducing the sentence by half compared to the original judgment. It is reported that Gao still expressed dissatisfaction and intends to file a third appeal to the Supreme Court, hoping to escape punishment.

Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center Publishes "The Rural Movement of Today" 189

The Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center spares no effort in its contribution to publishing. Now, the center's first research report, "The Rural Movement of Today in China," has been published. The book was written by Mr. Kong Xuexiong, a researcher at the center, and it provides a very detailed account of the rural movements in various parts of the country over the past ten years. It includes detailed descriptions of experimental movements in various places, such as the work in Ding County, Zouping, and Zhenping. It also provides systematic discussions on the development of various rural construction theories, such as village governance theories, rural education, and local autonomy. All the descriptions are based on actual investigations and are not empty theories. At a time when rural revitalization is being highly promoted, this book is the best reference material for both those working in rural areas and researchers of rural issues. The content includes a general discussion of the meaning and conditions of the rural movement, rural construction in Shandong, the Ding County experimental work of the Chinese National Association of the Mass Education Movement, rural improvement projects and mass education in Jiangsu, the people's militia and autonomy in Zhenping in the bandit area, the rural credit cooperative undertakings in Hebei, the movement from Xiaozhuang School to the work-study groups, and the Xiaoshan Dongxiang autonomy under party-led governance, all of which are extremely brilliant. Finally, it summarizes the gains and losses of the work in various places and his personal opinions. It covers the general trends of the rural reconstruction movement in China in recent years, as well as the works that can be called representative works, almost without omission. In addition, there is a preface by Mr. Sun Zhesheng and three appendices, including a survey of national rural improvement projects and a directory of rural movement workers, which are also relatively complete. The entire book contains more than 240,000 words, bound in a thick volume, priced at one yuan and five jiao. It is sold at major bookstores such as the Commercial Press, the Author Bookstore, and the Modern Bookstore. The publisher is the Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center on Avenue Foch, Shanghai.

Private Shipping Industry Meets to Assist After "Jing'an" Steamer is Detained, Decides to Petition the Government for Release 190

The "Jing'an" steamer of the Sanbei Steamer Company, which operates on the Shanghai-Hankou line, has been detained for more than 40 days since Yu Shicheng accused it of sinking a small steamer from Fuzhou and requested the court to impound it, resulting in significant losses. Moreover, the company's manager, Yu Qiaqing, believes that the sinking of the small steamer from Fuzhou was not caused by the "Jing'an" steamer at all. The Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau's Ship Collision Dispute Resolution Committee conducted a detailed investigation of the case, collecting witness testimonies and material evidence, and determined that the collision was not caused by the "Jing'an" steamer. Now, private shipping companies are outraged by the innocent detention of the "Jing'an" steamer, fearing that this will lead to a situation where everyone feels insecure. They have decided to convene a meeting in the coming days to discuss and petition the government for its release, and they will not stop until their goal is achieved.

Zhang Shunsheng Dares to Attack with a Chisel After Undermining Agreed-Upon Prices Among Competitors, Sentenced to Seven Months in Prison 191

Zhang Shunsheng, a native of Changzhou, runs a rubber stamp and ox-horn handle workshop at No. 100 Ziyoufang, Guangdong Road. Zhang Bingqing also runs the Yongxing Bookstore on Wangping Street. Previously, due to business competition, they had convened fellow merchants to agree on a uniform price of one jiao and two fen per ox-horn handle, which was not to be discounted. However, Zhang Shunsheng recently suddenly reduced the price to seven fen and seven li, which is more than three fen and five li lower than the agreed-upon price. Zhang Bingqing learned of this and, at 8:20 PM last night, led his shop assistants Liu Xingsheng and Li Delin to Zhang Shunsheng's place to reason with him, inviting him to a teahouse to discuss the matter. Unexpectedly, Zhang Shunsheng, knowing he was in the wrong, used a chisel from his workshop to stab Zhang Bingqing's thigh and both arms five times, all the way through, causing him to fall to the ground immediately. When Liu Xingsheng stepped forward to stop him, he was also stabbed in the eyebrow and chest. Zhang Shunsheng, realizing he had caused trouble, begged Liu and Zhang not to report him to the police, offering to send them to the hospital for treatment, with all medical expenses to be borne by him. He then took Liu and Zhang to Renji Hospital for treatment. The hospital notified the Laozha Police Station, which dispatched Detective Wang Yifei to arrest Zhang Shunsheng and detain him at the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court's Criminal Division One. The police lawyer, Li Zhishan, explained the case and filed charges under Article 294 of the Criminal Law. Zhang Bingqing recounted the situation at the time, saying, "I fainted three times yesterday after being stabbed, and the pain is unbearable." When questioned, the defendant confessed that he was slapped in the face by the plaintiffs and his front teeth were loosened, causing him to become disoriented, which led to the disaster. Judge Feng Shide, after verifying the confession, sentenced Zhang Shunsheng to seven months in prison for using a method sufficient to cause serious injury to harm another person.

Reading and Answering Questions

Knowledge Required for Work: Reading Guidance 198

I sincerely request your guidance for the knowledge required for my work.

My current position is equivalent to a library administrator, but with a different title. Therefore, I would like to acquire some knowledge about "statistics," "classification," and "cataloging." I wonder if there are any books on this subject? Which bookstores publish them? Please give me a detailed answer.

Also, I would like to study printing techniques in my spare time. I wonder if there are any magazines or books in China that specialize in printing? Please also give me instructions. I would be very grateful!

丨Letter from Xu Zhusan丨

Knowledge required for work is the most practical knowledge. I think this kind of demand is certainly not limited to Mr. Xu alone, and this aspect of social guidance has always been neglected. This column has rarely discussed this kind of problem before, but it is not that we have not paid attention to it. In fact, it is very difficult to answer these very common questions. In the past, we had not found talents in many fields. For example, once a painter asked us some chemical questions, and we could not find anyone to answer them, so we often could not satisfy the readers' wishes. This time, Mr. Xu's question about library knowledge has come to our own home.

However, before we discuss the practical knowledge needed in this kind of work, we must first understand what kind of department his work is in. What kind of difficulties are encountered in the specific work? What are the specific contents and scope? If there is no boundary, our answers will be difficult to start.

The questions raised by Mr. Xu seem to us to be vague, general, and abstract. Although he mentioned "statistics," "classification," and "cataloging," he did not point out any narrower scope of these questions. Therefore, we can only write something based on our general understanding of library science below...

1. Classification is the most arduous task in a library, which is generally acknowledged. The meaning of book classification is what is generally called "putting things of the same quality together." However, at first glance, this seems to have a clear meaning and no difficulty, but in fact, it often happens that a book can be classified into two or three or more categories. When encountering this kind of divergence and ambiguity, it often takes a lot of time to think hard, so doing this work sometimes makes people impatient because they cannot get the most appropriate category. But sometimes, you will also feel happy and interested in it. However, even though we say this, there are always principles and experiences to follow in handling any matter. Let us cite three points below: (1) Since there is no absolute scientific category for book classification, we can use theory as the basis on the one hand, and facts as the premise on the other hand, and integrate the two in the middle. The only thing we need to do is to make the books convenient to use. Then, it is possible to sacrifice a little academic law. For example, electrical engineering in natural science and electrical engineering in applied technology, the former is about the principles of electricity in natural science; the latter is about the technology of electricity in applied technology. According to theory, the two examples mentioned above should be given two categories, but if there are not many collections, and at the same time, in order to refer to a certain problem and avoid scattering, it is very reasonable to summarize them in one category. (2) When determining the category of each book, try to take the higher meaning. For example, if there is a book about the "May 30th Incident," this book can be divided into Sino-Japanese and Sino-British diplomatic issues, or it can be divided into modern Chinese history, but it is definitely not as great as the meaning of being divided into the Chinese national liberation revolutionary movement. (3) The order of classification has considerable significance, and this point must also be based on academic laws as much as possible. For example, if there are several books about the history of social thought, it is necessary to consider the order of occurrence and not to reverse the order.

The three items mentioned above are the general key arguments of the classification method. At the same time, it is too short to write about this aspect of academic theory here, and we cannot list them one by one. As for the question of which method to use for classification, we generally agree with the Dewey Decimal System because it has flexibility. If the library is small and there are not many books, it only needs to use the outline. If the scale is large and there are many books, the outline and detailed items can be used together. If the outline and detailed items are still not enough, decimal points can be added.

(2) Cataloging is a more complete work after the classification work in the library. With a complete catalog in the library, readers can use the guidance of the catalog to retrieve the information they want in their minds. However, this cataloging is the most practical and must rely on practice to understand. Moreover, the cataloging depends entirely on the needs and simplification of the library to determine the work. Some libraries only make a book title catalog, and some libraries also have an author catalog, subject catalog, classification catalog, and even a dictionary catalog. However, most libraries usually have two catalogs: book title and author. There are many rules for the cataloging method, and it is difficult to list them in fact. Fortunately, there is a special book introduction below, so I will not repeat it here.

(3) We also think that the problem of statistics is similar to the situation of cataloging, that is, how to count the materials generated in the work that Mr. Xu proposed. This all depends on the actual needs. As for the principles and methods of statistics, the following books can be used for reference.

(4) Regarding magazines and books specializing in printing technology, we have not heard of them in China. Recently, the Commercial Press's Publishing Weekly has a column "Common Sense of Printing" from the 75th issue, which is also worth reading. Today, the newspaper reported that the Commercial Press published a book on modern printing technology, priced at four jiao. We specially went to buy and read it. It is said that it is still their maiden work. These little things may slightly fill your desire for printing knowledge.

Attached book list

Academic Trends (Anhui Provincial Library, in the former prefectural government office, Anqing) 6. Chinese Publication Monthly (Zhejiang Circulation Library, Gulou, Hangzhou)

The 5th Shanghai Municipal People's Amateur Games will be held today at the Municipal No. 1 Public Sports Field. Sports will begin at 7:30 AM, and all athletes and referees must be present on time. The opening ceremony will be held at 8:00 AM, and Mayor Wu will personally deliver the opening speech. The preliminary rounds for the 800 meters, 200 meters, and 3000 meters were completed yesterday in the dim twilight. Those who score points in this event will be awarded a medal each. Details are as follows:

Far East Games North China Athletes Left Hong Kong Yesterday Morning for Return North; Yesterday South China Football Team Lost to Western Union 3-0 213

(Hong Kong, 26th) The Far East Games North China athletes left Hong Kong on the President Jackson this morning to return north. Only South China athletes remained in the football team. They played against the Western Union team at the South China Stadium at 5:30 PM, resulting in a 3-0 victory for the Western Union team.

(Central News Agency, 26th, Hong Kong) The Chinese Far East Games delegation, consisting of over 80 people led by Wang Zhengting, left Hong Kong by the original Jackson ship at 8:00 AM on the 26th to return north. Many representatives from various organizations went to the port to see them off.

(Central News Agency, 26th, Hong Kong) The Chinese Far East Games football team played a friendly match against the Western Union team at the Hong Kong Club Stadium at 5:30 PM on the afternoon of the 26th. Li Huitang and Feng Jingxiang were absent due to other engagements, which greatly reduced their strength. The players were tired from the journey, resulting in poor coordination. As a result, Western Union won 3-0.

Xiangbin Cup Table Tennis: Guangdong Champion; Jiande Absent from Final 217

The 7th Xiangbin Cup Table Tennis Tournament was held as scheduled last night at the Meifeng Table Tennis Room. Previously, the presidium of the cup tournament organizing committee, in view of the previous request to postpone the final, which had a significant impact, sent letters to both the Guangdong and Jiande teams the day before yesterday, stating that if they were absent from the final, they would be dealt with in accordance with Article 7, Paragraph 9 of the cup tournament rules on "withdrawal midway." Unexpectedly, three hours before the final, letters were received from both teams requesting a postponement of the competition, the reason being a conflict with the Chinese team's preliminary selection time (according to the so-called Chinese team preliminary selection, it is said that it is being prepared for the "Far East Sino-Japanese Table Tennis Competition" to be held next month). The committee immediately replied, stating that all matters had been arranged long ago, and it would be difficult to comply with the request to postpone the competition. It also explained that now that the Far East Games have been illegally dissolved, even the Sino-Japanese tennis exhibition match has been canceled, so why bother with table tennis? Therefore, it hoped that they would still attend on time. When the final came, the Guangdong team indeed understood the greater good and attended in full, while the Jiande team, except for the captain Lu Zhongqiu, all were absent. The referee Zhou Weixin announced that Jiande had forfeited the match, and the representative of the cup tournament organizing committee explained the circumstances, stating that it should be considered a withdrawal midway, and all their competition results in this tournament should be canceled. Therefore, this year's championship was won by the Guangdong team. The runners-up were promoted in order, with Tianma and Meifeng teams tied for second place, each receiving a pennant as encouragement. Ms. Shi Shuming presented the awards on the spot, followed by a happy banquet and refreshments.

China Table Tennis Association Rejects Japanese Team's Visit to Shanghai for Competition; Preliminary Selection Still Held as Usual 218

The Shanghai China Table Tennis Association, because the China-Japan International Table Tennis Championship was scheduled to be held in Shanghai, China in early June, held preliminary selections for the Chinese team on the evening of the 23rd of this month in order to select true talent. However, since this year's Far East Games were undermined by the Japanese, people across the country were outraged. The Japanese side wanted to fulfill its long-cherished wish to participate with its pseudo-nation, and used its so-called ghost tactics of illegally producing the East Asia Amateur Sports Association, which is not worth a smile from knowledgeable people. It is now learned that the association is indignant about the unreasonable undermining of the Far East Games by the Japanese, so it has decided to send a telegram to Japan rejecting the visit to Shanghai for the competition. As for the preliminary selection of the Chinese team, which is a regular association affair that the association should hold, it will still be held as usual to assess the skills of each individual.

▲Sports Performance... Tonight

The Southeast Women's Physical Education Teachers' School 10th Anniversary Celebration will hold a sports performance tonight (the 27th). The program is extensive and the performances are novel. All kinds of costumes and clothing are made by the students of the school themselves. Therefore, preparations have been extremely busy recently. ▲Approved the Petition to Establish Labor Education Experimental Zones

(Nanjing, 26th) The Committee for the Design of Labor Education under the Ministries of Industries and Education held a meeting on the 25th. The most important resolution was to petition the two ministries to establish labor education experimental zones, and to designate Shanghai, Wuxi, Qingdao, Tianjin, Hankou, and other places to conduct pilot programs first, in order to promote the labor education plan. This proposal was discussed for the longest time, and the result was its approval. The draft organizational charter for the labor education experimental zones attached to the original proposal was also revised and approved. Other matters, such as the proposal to establish labor education implementation committees in industrially developed areas, the proposal to petition the two ministries to organize a committee for the compilation of labor education materials, the proposal to petition the two ministries to appoint responsible personnel to inspect, guide, and supervise the designated labor education experimental zones, the proposal to emphasize labor education in urban social education implementation agencies and to establish special labor education implementation agencies in cities, and the editing and issuance of labor songs, were all separately revised and approved.

Junior High Student from Provincial Nanjing Middle School Drowns While Swimming 227

Zhou Gao, a 19-year-old student in the Junior High School Class A of the Provincial Nanjing Middle School's Second Academy, a native of Jiangning County, Jiangsu Province, went to exercise on the playground as usual after school at 4:00 PM on the 25th of this month (the playground of the school's Second Academy is outside the school walls, which are very low, and recently they were knocked down by outsiders, making it very easy to climb out). When it was time for self-study at 7:00 PM, the student was missing. While they were searching for him, Chen Ju and other students from Anhui Middle School reported to the school that Zhou Gao was swimming in the swimming pool outside Tongji Gate near the Jiulong Bridge and suddenly disappeared. Upon hearing this, the junior high school director immediately instructed the regular supervisor and the student's homeroom teacher, Zhou Zhongchen, and physical education teacher Li Kehang, along with six other faculty members, to rush to the scene. At the same time, they reported to the principal (at the First Academy). After the homeroom teacher and others arrived at the Jiulong Bridge, they immediately hired local bailiff Wang Hong to hire people to retrieve the body. After about half an hour, they managed to pull the student ashore. His limbs were already stiff, and his abdomen had caved in. Li Kehang tried to use artificial respiration to resuscitate him, but it was ineffective. They then ordered the bailiff to guard the body and dispatched four more school workers from the school to jointly watch over it. Upon hearing the news, the principal immediately went to the Second Academy and sent someone with a letter to the student's home in Xijiao Village, Chunhua Town, outside Tongji Gate, to inform his parents. Three supervisors from the Provincial Department of Education happened to be in Nanjing to inspect the school and were residing in the Second Academy, so they reported the situation to the provincial supervisors and telegraphed the Department of Education. They also separately reported to the Ninth Police Precinct and requested the Jiangning District Court to send personnel to conduct an autopsy.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

How Should Students Practice the New Life Movement? 235

— Bo Zhen

"New Life, New Life!" What a fashionable slogan. The purpose of the New Life Movement is: to build the nation and revive the people! To improve the knowledge and morality of the people! To enable the general public to have neat, clean, simple, and plain clothing, food, housing, and transportation. To conform to the virtues of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame! It can be seen that the purpose of the New Life Movement is so significant! So important!

We students are the masters of the future nation, and the responsibility of saving the country rests on our shoulders. We are the vanguard of practicing the New Life Movement, so we should understand how to practice the New Life Movement.

The most important points are roughly the following two:

(1) Rules: We must abide by the rules as human beings, so there is also a rule in the rules of the New Life Movement. When you meet someone in the morning, you should say "Good morning." When you say goodbye, say "Goodbye." As the saying goes, "Greeting people doesn't cost anything, just a roll of the tongue." When eating, do not have rash movements. Walk on the left side. There are many rules, too numerous to list.

(2) Cleanliness: Cleanliness is the key to longevity, so there is also cleanliness in the articles of the New Life Movement. Clothes should be washed often, windows should be opened often, nails should be cut often, and hair should be combed often.

I think someone will definitely say, "There are so many rules, and it is so difficult and troublesome to implement them one by one." In fact, what is so difficult about this? Why be afraid of trouble? As long as you practice one or two items every day, you will be practicing the New Life Movement in less than one or two months.

Little friends, I think you really must not be afraid of difficulties and troubles.

The Story of May 236

— Ding He

One night in May, when Yingdi and Lanmei were fighting for a piece of cake, Dad came back from outside. When they saw Dad, they dropped the cake and went up to call him.

Dad just smiled at them and sat down on a chair next to him. Then, he called them to sit beside him and called me to sit beside him.

Dad first asked his brother what month it was now.

Yingdi quickly said "May". Dad asked Lanmei again, and Lanmei also quickly said "May". Dad asked me again.

"May is May, but we should call it National Humiliation Month."

After I finished speaking, Dad nodded and said, "That's right." But Yingdi and Lanmei were surprised. At this time, Dad sighed and said:

"Just remembering, not thinking about avenging humiliation, is no longer what we should do. Not only do you not think about avenging humiliation, but you don't even remember."

So Yingdi and Lanmei cried. At this time, Dad laughed again and told them the story of May in detail from beginning to end.

After Dad finished telling the story of May, Yingdi said, "We want to unite the children of China, stand up together to avenge humiliation, stand up together to avenge humiliation."

Sibling Rivalry 237

— Hu Yunwu

One day, the hands and feet were arguing about which was more noble and which was more lowly. The hand scolded the foot and said, "There is nothing more lowly than your 'foot' in the world. Why is that? First, your soles are always treading on the ground and never see the light of day. Second, if your face 'foot' is lifted up for people to see, people will scold you for not knowing respect." The foot laughed and said, "When I am dirty, isn't it your 'hand' that washes my feet? If you want to pick something up, can you get it if I refuse to move?" The hand was questioned by the foot and was rendered speechless. The foot then said, "There is no distinction between noble and lowly in the world. Each has its own use. We must help each other to be effective."

Animal Feet 238

— Chi Fo

Little friends! It is very interesting to study various animals, big and small. Just from their 'feet,' they are already in all shapes and colors, very interesting.

Land animals all have feet. The feet of aquatic animals are turned into fins. Some have webs on their feet. Why is this? Because animals that walk on land need feet to walk, and animals in the water need fins or webs to swim. This is all because they are adapting to the environment.

The feet of fierce beasts have claws for tearing and devouring other animals. The soles of their feet have thick flesh, so they make no sound when they walk and do not get hurt when they jump. The feet of carnivores such as tigers, leopards, cats, and lions are all like this. Clumsy beasts have hooves on their feet, some with double hooves and some with single hooves. So, hoofed animals are divided into two types: even-toed and odd-toed. Animals such as elephants, cattle, and sheep are hoofed animals.

Birds are flying animals, with feet and claws. Insects all have six legs. Ducks are good at swimming and have webs on their feet; so do frogs. They are like oars for sailing a boat. The pectoral fins and ventral fins of fish are like oars, and the tail fin is like a rudder. It's really interesting.

Snakes, roundworms, pinworms, and tapeworms have no feet and move entirely by wriggling their bodies. The hind legs of frogs and deer are long and their front legs are short, so they jump extremely fast. Crabs have eight legs. Giraffes丨Perhaps this is what the ancients called 'Qilin'丨Their necks are too high and they all walk sideways. The front two legs of birds have turned into wings, so they can fly.

— Zhang Yuming

Cuckoo! Cuckoo!
