You are worthy of being a beneficial bird!

Stevenson's Childhood 240

— Lin Ruan

Little friends, do you know the great British inventor Stevenson? The train you see was invented by him. He was the son of a coal company stoker. When he was young, he only herded sheep for others. At the age of fourteen, he helped his father with work. But he was secretly reading at the same time. Later, his father died, and the whole family's clothes were all borne by him alone. At that time, he also lost his wife, and his sadness cannot be described.

But Stevenson, who was not afraid of difficulties, regardless of whether his ability was sufficient, began to study science. The first time he invented the safety lamp in coal mines, and the second time, he invented the train, a tool of transportation. He publicly demonstrated it on the road from Liverpool to Manchester, and the people who watched cheered and wished him success, but he died in 1848.

Little friends, people who struggle, even if the environment is bad, cannot be stopped.

A Letter to Little Friends in the City 241

— Xu Zongjie

Dear Little Friends:

Your innocence, liveliness, and happiness are so enviable, so I gave up the qualification of an old man 丨丨I am nearly forty years old 丨丨and hang out with you kids all day long, being the oldest little brother.

Little friends! I now live in the countryside, and I can also be called an old little brother in the countryside. What are some of the scenes in the countryside in early summer? What do we play? Let me report some to you.

The rice seedlings in the field are already two inches long, planted in rows and columns. The rapeseed flowers have already formed seeds, the peas have also formed fruit. A kind of small bird is calling, "Plant quickly! Plant quickly!" The strong young men in the village have begun to bare their legs, roll up their sleeves, and go down to the fields to work.

My little friends and I get up together at 5:00 in the morning, walking and jumping on the banks of the fields. There is some dew on the grass, and the eastern sun is beginning to show its crimson face. We look at the rice seedlings in the field, look at the tadpoles in the stream, and listen to the birds singing on the branches. After walking like this for an hour, we each go home to have breakfast, go to school, and do work.

Dusk is our happiest time. A large, soft, green lawn is our playground and natural chair. Many little friends are kicking balls on it, or racing and high jumping. We pick many wildflowers and braid them into crowns to give to the winners. When we are tired of playing, we lie on it, telling stories and singing folk songs, until the sun sinks in the west, and Mr. Toad, who shouts slogans, dismisses the meeting, and we each go home.

Little friends! How do you feel about these simple reports? Would you like to try this country life? I welcome you to join us, I wish you happiness. Your old little brother Xu Zongjie, greetings.

What Does the Earth Look Like? 242

— Han Yu

Little friends! Do you know what the Earth looks like?

The shape of the Earth is a sphere. To be more precise, its shape is like an orange. If little friends don’t believe the Earth is round, you can go to the seaside and look at a ship coming from afar. First, we see the ship's smokestack, and only later can we see the body of the ship. If you think the Earth is flat, we should see the body and the smokestack together. How can this phenomenon occur?

During a lunar eclipse, we can see a round shadow on the moon. This shadow is the Earth's shadow reflected onto the moon. The dark shadow is round, so of course, the Earth is also round.

Little friends may ask, "The Earth is round and constantly moving. Why don't we feel it at all?" You can catch an ant and put it on a ball, and quickly spin the ball. But the ant can still walk forward without feeling anything. This is because the ball is too big, and the ant is too small. We are like many ants, and the Earth is a huge ball.

About Grabbing Thirty 243

— Sheng Huai

Little friends! Last time, this publication featured the "Grabbing Thirty" mini-game. You must have played it already. I want to ask you, what experiences did you gain after playing?

Little friends! I will now write down the experience of "Grabbing Thirty" here. Do you want to know?

Step 1: Within ten, grab three, six, nine.

Step 2: Above ten, within twenty, grab two, five, eight.

Step 3: Above twenty, within thirty, grab one, four, seven.

With this method of grabbing, you are guaranteed to get thirty. If you don't believe it, try it!

Sending Eggs 丨Sensory Game丨 244

— Yin

Whether a child's sense of feeling is acute or not is significantly related to innate physiology, but postnatal behavioral training is also very important. If a naturally dull and insensitive child is given proper training, although they cannot catch up with a gifted child, they can at least surpass children who have not received sensory training. The best training method is through games. This "Sending Eggs" game is one of the methods to train children's sensory acuity.

There is no limit to the number of people playing the game, but too few will reduce interest, and too many will make guessing difficult, so the most appropriate number is five to ten people. The location of the game is not limited; it can be indoors or outdoors. Before starting, first select one person to be the "egg sender" and one person to be the "guesser." The remaining people stand with their hands behind their backs, leaning against a wall. The guesser closes their eyes tightly and stands about ten steps away from the people leaning against the wall. The egg sender prepares a small rubber ball or a pebble to represent the egg. They can sing, "Chicken Mama is sending eggs, who wants them? Who wants them?" While giving the egg to any child, they then say, "It's sent! Guess who got it, and I'll give it to you to eat!" The guesser then walks closer to the children standing against the wall, observes their expressions, and guesses who received the egg. If they guess correctly, the person who received the egg and the guesser switch roles. If they guess incorrectly, they try again. If they guess incorrectly three times, they are penalized by singing a song or telling a story. The egg sender can switch or give away the egg multiple times before finally giving it to someone. The children who received the egg or did not receive the egg can deliberately make peculiar expressions to make it difficult for the guesser to observe.

Magpies and Crows 245

— Da Qi

A magpie's call brings good news, and a crow's caw brings misfortune. This is a superstition. Magpies and crows are birds. How can they know a person's fortune? However, some people know that it is not credible, but when they hear a magpie calling, they can't help but feel happy; when they hear a crow cawing, they can't help but feel disgusted. In fact, crows know how to feed their parents, they are filial birds, and not something very bad. But people always curse them whenever they open their mouths, it's really unfair to them. However, the crow's caw, "wa wa wa," carries a sorrowful sound, causing people to feel unhappy and somewhat dislike listening to it. If the crow is ignorant of this and nods its head at people, cawing constantly, they will pick up stones and throw them to drive it away. Isn't this what we often see? Although a magpie's call is not particularly good, it is relatively energetic and pleasant to listen to, so it is okay if it calls a little. There is no harm if it calls a lot. It is always welcomed everywhere.

Little friends, from the above, we can see that people's speech must also be appropriate. Compositions have grammar, writing characters has character rules, painting has painting methods, how can speaking not have methods? In ancient times, elementary schools had "rules for responding," which studied speech. Sage's schools had a "speech subject," which also emphasized speech. If speech is not done properly, no matter how good your knowledge and character are, you will easily provoke resentment and jealousy whenever you speak, and you will encounter obstacles everywhere, just like a crow, making people disgusted when it opens its mouth. How can you gain a foothold in society?

How to Draw a Black Cat 248

— Wu Song Bao

Umbrellas of the Past Three Thousand Years: Ancient and Modern 249

— He Gongchao

(1) Egyptian Umbrellas (2) Assyrian Umbrellas on Two-Wheeled Chariots (3) Assyrian Noble Umbrellas (4) Greek Umbrellas (5) Roman Umbrellas (6) Ancient Chinese Umbrellas (7) Siamese Noble Umbrellas (8) Japanese Umbrellas (9) Ashanti Umbrellas (10) Sandar People's Umbrella Dance (11) Modern Umbrellas

Umbrellas have existed since ancient times, and they were a symbol of authority used by monarchs and nobles. In the engravings and patterns of ancient Egypt and Assyria, we can see a servant holding an umbrella for a monarch, which shows that he is a person of authority. Umbrellas spread from the above two places to Greece and Rome, but they became tools for shielding from the sun. However, in Eastern countries, even now, umbrellas are still regarded as a symbol of authority, such as in Siam, Malaya, and places like Ashanti and Abyssinia in Africa. In ancient China, umbrellas also contained a solemn and noble meaning. But in modern times, they are only used as tools for sheltering from rain and sun, or as decorations for women. In Japan, the situation is the same as in China.

Women's World

Regarding Daycares and Public Childcare 250

— Zi Jiu

Since the news of establishing "daycares" in Shanghai, it has attracted general attention. In the supplement to this newspaper on May 13th, there was an article by Mr. Shi Shi, "Regarding Daycares and Public Childcare." It was against daycares, and the general idea was: "Although public childcare in European and American countries has been implemented and achieved results, given the current social conditions, national economy, cultural level, and family concepts in our country, it is believed that there are still doubts about promoting public childcare." The reasons for opposing it are roughly based on two points: (1) Opposing women engaging in occupations and neglecting childcare. (2) Suspecting public childcare itself.

Regarding the first point, Mr. Shi Shi said: "The current engagement of ordinary Chinese women in occupations is actually just selling short-term youth... After marriage, society cannot reserve considerable positions for mothers with children, then daycares naturally lose their necessity of existence. Moreover, women have the natural duty of raising children. Raising children to make them physically and mentally healthy is serving society, and its value is greater than being a vase in an organization or a living signboard in a commercial market." The need for women to engage in occupations, even if we abandon ideological theories, just talking about the current situation in China, due to years of imperialist aggression, the brink of internal strife, rural bankruptcy, and market depression, middle- and lower-class housewives have had no choice but to seek occupations to make a living. Among women from middle- and upper-class families, they have had the opportunity to receive education. Once they have knowledge and skills, they will naturally want to develop their instincts and engage in politics, academics, or other occupations to do what they can. Therefore, women's engagement in occupations is an inevitable phenomenon in the current society. Since there are working women on one hand, there is a need for childcare institutions on the other hand. One side can concentrate on work, and the other side can provide high-quality education. Those who like to work can work, and those who like to educate children can educate children. It can be said to be a division of labor for individuals and cooperation for society. As for the so-called engaging in occupations is just selling short-term youth, it is indeed a derogatory term for working women. But we cannot deny that many working women do give up their occupations after marriage or can no longer engage in occupations. The former is caused by the phenomenon of a society with too few opportunities. The reasons for the latter are varied, but it is also due to the lack of childcare institutions.

Regarding the second point, Mr. Shi Shi believes that public childcare will destroy family bonds, so he says: "Children and families have an inseparable relationship. Children are the center of family happiness... Having children and grandchildren around the knees constitutes family harmony... Family is also a paradise for children. Parental love is the only nourishment for children's lives, otherwise, it is difficult to survive." Mr. Shi Shi is still dreaming of that kind of feudalistic peaceful paradise of having children and grandchildren around the knees. In fact, in the current society where life is busy and making a living is not easy, it is impossible for middle- and lower-class families to enjoy this leisurely family harmony. Moreover, daycares are different from China's inherent orphanages. Children raised in daycares still have to go home on time to reunite with their parents. As for whether the family is a paradise for children, it is questionable. The fact is that ordinary Chinese families are a hell for children. The rich do not know how to teach or raise them, only knowing how to spoil them; the poor cannot even talk about raising them. Moreover, Chinese children are accustomed to family life and lack group cultivation. The habit of being like scattered sand is half formed by family life. As for parental love, it is indeed the spiritual nourishment for children, but doting love and selfish love—parents see children as playthings and private property—loving them appropriately harms them, not only harming the children themselves but also causing harm to society. The high mortality rate of Chinese children is unparalleled. The reasons are varied, but it is also due to the inability to teach, the inability to raise them, and the result of hunger and cold. In this situation, there is a need for public and more scientific methods of education.

Regarding the charging of fees, according to the general practice in advanced countries, it is mostly proportional to the income of the young children's parents and is not related to the number of children.

Mr. Shi Shi said at the end: "In fact, it only provides a convenient door for frivolous playboys to indulge in pleasure, and the result may become the final destination for illegitimate children and adulterous children." In recent years, the rampant spread of human desires has been a well-known fact. Then the proliferation of illegitimate children and adulterous children may be an inevitable phenomenon. This bad phenomenon is a social illness. Illegitimate children or adulterous children are inherently innocent. Moreover, the Chinese nation used to have 400 million people, but now it may be less than that number. For the sake of reviving the nation, I believe that whether they are illegitimate children or legitimate children, it is necessary to find ways to make them grow up healthy. Therefore, I am glad that Shanghai will soon have daycares. I hope that more and more daycares will be established in cities and towns. However, I hope that those who run daycares will strive for scientific methods, avoid being aristocratic, and make it more convenient for poor children.

Opinions of Great Thinkers on Women's Issues (8) 251

— Hua

Seven Owen

Owen (Robert Owen) was a great British utopian socialist, born in 1771 and died in 1858. At this time, the progress of technology in British production had turned a large number of skilled craftsmen into appendages of machines or completely excluded from production and replaced by unskilled weak women and children, which was the period of "rampant evil" of capitalism. Whole batches of young children died from being cruelly exploited in factories. Owen was born in this era and witnessed all kinds of tragedies, which made him transform from a great industrialist and humanitarian into a thorough social reformer.

The scope of his social reform was very broad, including protecting children, running education, setting up schools, establishing daycares, protecting factory labor, opening hospitals, and providing relief to the elderly and the unemployed. In order to realize his ideals, Owen attempted to establish a communist commune to replace the old and dying system. But he did not understand that the economic liberation of workers and escape from slavery must be the matter of the workers themselves. Owen believed that the "wise and far-sighted people" of all parties could jointly achieve the necessary reforms.

When Owen was ten years old, his father ordered him to be an apprentice in a rural shop. Later, he worked in the two major cities of London and Manchester for several years. In 1790, Owen, at the age of nineteen, became the manager of a large spinning mill in Manchester (which was then the center of the British textile industry). Seven years later, he joined with friends and bought a spinning mill in New Lanark, Scotland, for 1.25 million marks, with three thousand male and female workers and children. This factory became the testing ground for his social reform plan.

Owen's first task was to pay attention to children. He set up many daycares to reduce the burden of female workers with children. He abolished the method of rewarding and punishing children in the schools he ran; his factory also did not hire children under the age of ten to work: those over the age of ten were required to work for twelve and a half hours, which was a huge progress at the time, because even a four-year-old child had to work in the factory for twelve to sixteen hours.

In 1825, in order to realize his ideal of a new social system, Owen purchased a piece of land in Indiana, USA, and established a communist community called "New Harmony." Owen had many outstanding male and female comrades here, among whom a Ms. Bright played a particularly important role in the women's movement. She personally established a small group within "New Harmony." After the failure of the "New Harmony" experiment, Ms. Bright continued to fight for many years to fight for women's equality.

Owen believed that women are born equal to men and have no obligation to obey men. He also bravely implemented his beliefs in life, although this caused violent attacks on him by society, he was still unyielding. In "New Harmony," women enjoyed the right to vote and to be elected. In the "Young America" magazine run by his son, he published his twelve demands, one of which was "men and women should be completely equal."

Owen deeply believed in the power of mankind's highest ideals. He attempted to create a new, more perfect, and collective social life system as an example to resist the brutal exploitation of the time. In all aspects, he revealed a wealth of ideas, which were the object of ridicule and sarcasm at the time, but are now the treasures of international socialism.

As for Owen's opinions on marriage, prostitution, women's occupations, and children's education, let's talk about them next time.

Meticulous Charm Movement and Women's Liberation 252

— Jiong

A meticulous charm movement has recently been advocated in Cleveland, USA.

It is said that the rise of this meticulous charm movement is based on pleasing men. Because men feel that: a woman with makeup is simply a vase, without a soul, only for people to play with. This not only fails to show a lively posture but also has adverse effects on health: how can it be called "a gentleman's good match"? Therefore, they stood on the position of pleasing men and found: (1) Because the number of women with tuberculosis is increasing, it is not easy to prevent disease and prolong life without advocating the meticulous charm movement. (2) Developing meticulous charm is also an opportunity for women to exercise their bodies, making their bodies healthier day by day, and diseases cannot invade. (3) Women decorating their faces with powder is not considered beautiful. They must have a charming posture to be fully beautiful. (4) They must work hard on meticulous charm, and then they can be pursued by men everywhere. These are the reasons for launching the meticulous charm movement: holding lectures everywhere, posting slogans, and even each women's group has an affiliated meticulous charm training school, educating them to charm men, to charm their lovers, to charm their husbands, as well as narrative charm, love charm, greeting charm, farewell charm, walking charm, etc., so that they become experts in pleasing men. Can it be said that this can be beneficial to the women's liberation movement?

We know that the reason why women are in an oppressed position is due to social systems and economic conditions. We can understand the ins and outs of this as long as we turn over the history of social evolution and the history of women's liberation movement. But the ladies of America are turning a new trick after getting tired of the taste of powder: they fully believe that working hard on meticulous charm, being pursued by men everywhere, showing their health and arrogance, is liberation (?!) This is simply a self-deceiving joke!

If we think that things from the West are always "modern" and learn this meticulous charm, then our 200 million women under double oppression will not only disarm themselves but also cancel the camp of fighting for liberation. Because this meticulous charm movement presents us with a posture of pleasing men. It is a huge stone blocking the path of the women's liberation movement. It is a cup of anesthetic soup. Therefore, we should resolutely block the invasion of this meticulous charm movement and strengthen our women's movement front, and strive to fight from the economic and political aspects, and then we can obtain true liberation!

Do You Believe It? Twins Can Actually Have Two Fathers 253

— Wu

Not long ago, a strange case of twins being able to have two fathers occurred in South Dakota (S·Dakota) in the United States, causing a sensation in society, and the local court made a new precedent that had never been seen in the world for this matter. Readers, do you believe it? This is indeed true, because in Pullman Village in that state, there was a farmer named Yadwa Babad, who had two identical twins, one of whom looked very much like Babad, while the other did not look like Babad at all. So Babad was very suspicious. Because his wife had been having an affair with someone else, Babad obtained evidence, and then the dispute began. Babad said: He can only fulfill his father's obligation to his own child (that is, the one who looks like him). As for the other one, it is definitely not his child and can only be the responsibility of the mother. As a result, the couple quarreled in the state court. Naturally, Babad's reasons were very sufficient. After several interrogations by the court, Judge Duriber finally ruled in favor of Babad's request, and the couple were to be responsible for the support of the two children separately. In this way, can't twins really have two fathers?

Echoes of "A Woman's Heart" 254

— Jue

"You are wrong!"

Sir:

In the tenth issue of Women's World, your tragic history was published. At the end, you said, "Who is willing to tell me 'You are right' or 'You are wrong'?" According to my shallow knowledge to "criticize" (?), I can confidently say: "You are wrong!"

Please don't doubt that I am speaking against my conscience. I am defending my own gender.

First: I feel that when you are just starting to fall in love, you should naturally use all your abilities to observe your object. Aren't newspapers and magazines full of news about marriage deception now? Can you suddenly believe that your object will not be the protagonist in those news stories? Looking closely at your "A Woman's Heart," you don't seem to have noticed this.

Second: Since you knew that not long before you fell in love, he had been passionately in love with another woman; you should have explored why he broke up with his first lover and how he broke up with his first lover. Of course, he will use deceptive and improper means to break away from you, and his means of breaking away from his first lover must also be nothing more than deception or other improper methods. But according to you, you only know "It is said that she refused to agree to his request, and then they broke up."

He will break up with his first lover because she did not agree to his request. Can you guarantee that he will not break up with you because you do not agree to his request to love another woman?

Third: Since your friend warned you, "Can you believe that he will not fall in love with a third woman?" Why did you suddenly believe him? He will smash the precious lute that his teacher gave him, which shows that he is a guy who is good at forgetting friends. Those who write blood letters are often the most weak-willed people. People who use death to threaten others are the worst scum of mankind. You cannot be moved by his blood letter; you cannot abandon your doubts and hesitation for his "death." Death! Don't you know that many compatriots in the Northeast were brutally killed by the violent Japanese? Don't you know that many compatriots in the Northwest were drowned and starved to death by natural disasters? Don't you know that many round-headed and square-footed civilians were shot to death by military men? What is so great about the death of a person who would smash the precious lute that his teacher gave him and use it to deceive the love of the opposite sex!

Also fourth: You cannot hate your heart for not being "ruthless" and not being "poisonous." Your failure is not because your heart is not "ruthless" and not being "poisonous," but because your brain lacks rationality! Your heart is too easily moved.

With these four points, I dare to say that you are wrong. However, sir, you are a Hunanese, and Hunanese and Cantonese are the bravest, most enterprising, most revolutionary, and most hopeful people in our country. I respectfully wish you to use the blood of my Hunanese people to break through the obscurity of your future!

School Life Sketches: After-School Jottings 255

— Meng Kai

I am not one who resides in the school dormitory. Therefore, I wouldn't know about the novelties of the "East Palace" and "West Palace." This is merely about my everyday after-school activities.

We rarely have the chance to chat idly because, once the dismissal bell rings, everyone is busy packing their bags to go home. So, it is only when there are no classes or when the teacher is absent that...

People's personalities differ, so their actions are obviously quite different: diligent students, holding the motto of "an inch of time is worth an inch of gold," bury themselves in their books, but there are only one or two like that in the entire grade. Some active students happily skip rope and play basketball on the playground, fully expressing their liveliness and innocence. Students who are obsessed with movies and Cantonese opera gather to chat: "What? The movie premiering today is XX film, starring the newly chosen queen... It's a pity I don't have a chance to see it... That star is so pretty and charming. Chen Fei-nong's performance is just right... Chen Zhao-hong is so beautiful... Liang Shao-ping is so fat... The male cast's performance last night was great, a must-see!" They often talk like this with great interest, chattering away. Students who like to dress up always talk about the new fashions of 1934 and how to dress... "Today, to the Guanghan Palace, the Great Light..." "Electric wave... lover... stroll in the park..." There are many more, I can't remember them all. Some students with literary interests often play the old tune of the grayness of life... As for me, I don't talk much, and there's nothing to talk about. When I encounter such scenes, I just silently listen to their idle chatter, or take the opportunity to observe their personalities. So, I often sigh like this: "Alas! Today's female students are mostly immersed in dreams, besides food, clothing, shelter, reading, and entertainment. What do social affairs have to do with them?"

Smoke Screen 256

— Zi Gang

Youth, delicacy, and laughter.

All these are concealed behind a hollow and heavy curtain. Behind the curtain lurks a fierce and man-eating wolf, and the curtain-pullers are some foolish lackeys.

Opening their insatiable blood-bowls and waiting for the students' $, imparting some smoke-bomb knowledge and flattering skills, telling you to say one, and you can't say two, telling you to be calm, and even coughing is superfluous. If you obediently wag your tail, you might see a smile on the tiger's face. If you go crazy and want to take a breath and take a longer step, good:

"Crack!" A whip will lash you, a stern warning.

After the whip-like lecture, they will force you to participate in the provincial sports meet, write memorial essays for the school board, and submit articles for the "××××" essay contest. Why? To please their master. In front of the master, they themselves transform into slaves.

Foreign teachers host guests, and the girls dress up in colorful clothes to be guests. Of course, a few fluent conversational sentences are indispensable, but usually, it is forbidden to run outside, stopping at the triple gate, and you can't leave the school gate more than six times in half a year. The fear is that wandering around will distract you from your studies. On the other hand, they are vigorously advocating for the school to be a home and socialized: inviting parents to admire the spring scenery on campus. Thinking that their daughters and sisters are growing up in this good environment, the parents smile with relief, and there is no lack of praise: a good place to cultivate emotions and character.

It seems that "general customs" have caused the students to establish an autonomous association, approved by the school, supervising the executive committee and the general assembly. The selection of personnel is particularly concerning: those who are quiet and obedient, those who talk too much at meetings are troublemakers, especially "those clever people who still need to sort out the remaining or un-mailed donations."

Learning some waltzes or foxtrots in physical education is in line with the years of dancing to save the country! Twisting their waists, draped in puffy, wave-like hair, and with the pleasant sound of clattering leather shoes, the young women loosely feel the mystery of spring.

Only tricky lessons lock up the students' spring mood: monthly exams, major exams, plus the graduation examination. Cracking it is a must, otherwise the school has the right to deny participation in the graduation examination, fearing that bad grades will affect the school's overall average score. The authorities never forget to win the hearts of their masters.

Graduation is not easy. It is necessary to send 500 to 1,000 worth of souvenirs to the school, raise donations, but the girls frown. Everyone knows that the economic recession has affected families, and most families have been hit by this.

Thinking blankly, feeling resentful:

"This world is a mystery, when will the fighting end?"

Few can understand the causes and consequences of this contradiction and terror. It is just that the sheep are really suffering from tremor, and this disease is spreading.

Letters to the Editor 257

(1) To the esteemed editor: I have read the article "Our School" in the women's section of your newspaper on May 13th, which stated that the school prohibits reading "The Education of Love" and inspects hymens, and generally refers to the authorities' oppression of students. The editor's note at the end of the article declares that the article was submitted by a student from Qingdao Municipal Girls' Middle School, and the author claims responsibility. However, it is doubtful whether the content is fabricated, and we ask the local educational administrators to pay attention, which shows that your newspaper is concerned about women's education. However, the article is not a faithful record, and its attack on the school authorities is very obvious, especially the two sections that prohibit reading "The Education of Love" and inspect hymens, which are completely untrue. Now, I would like to inform the editor of your newspaper of the actual situation investigated by our bureau. This school pays great attention to the physical and mental education of students. Therefore, the school stipulates that teachers and staff should examine students' self-study reading materials at any time, and advise students not to read any books that are not suitable for the physical and mental cultivation of young people. As for the book "The Education of Love," it was originally on display in the school library, so how could it be prohibited from reading? Regarding physical examinations, as the editor said, the school regards it as one of the ways to promote students' health. Therefore, there are two types of examinations: disease examinations and physical examinations. The former is purely for the purpose of examining diseases and is carried out by the school doctor. The latter is mostly for the development of the body and is examined by physical education teachers and staff of the training office. This time, the physical examination was carried out by three female teachers, namely to examine whether the students' bodies were developing normally and whether their clothes and dresses were harmful to hygiene, and there was absolutely no inspection of the hymen. More than 300 students underwent the examination, and there was no coercion. The claims in the article are an exaggeration and sensationalization of the issue, and are probably not the work of the school's students. However, since the submission claims to be responsible for the content, your newspaper should (omission) make a factual correction to clarify the truth, and we look forward to your reply. This is addressed to the Shanghai Shenbao Newspaper, Qingdao Municipal Education Bureau, May 18th.

(2) To the esteemed editor: I have recently read the article "My School" published in the women's section of your newspaper on May 13th, which contains many defamatory and slanderous statements about our school, and claims that it was submitted by a student from our school, which is very shocking. Disease examinations are a routine event for our school every semester. This semester, on March 5th (Health Week), in addition to inviting Dr. Jiao, a school doctor, to give a lecture on "Health Issues" during Memorial Week, the disease examination began in the afternoon after class. It was carried out by the school doctor, with the assistance of nurses from the Municipal Hospital and staff from the training office. The examination included the ears, eyes, teeth, throat, and heart and lungs to check for diseases, and each item was entered into the disease examination form. The intention was to implement effective treatment or prevention based on the examination results to improve the health of the students. On March 7th, a physical examination was also held, which was carried out by a female physical education teacher, with the assistance of staff from the training office and a female English teacher. The examination included the posture of the head, shoulders, back, spine, abdomen, and feet, as well as the grip strength, and each item was entered into the physical examination form in order to implement appropriate corrections to achieve correct posture. This work was completed within three weeks. As for the "inspection of the hymen," not only has the gentleman "never heard of it before,"

Our school has never even thought of it, let alone implemented it! Other sections such as prohibiting the reading of "The Education of Love" are absurd and ridiculous, and there is no need to explain them. Rumors stop with the wise. As the gentleman said, "Although it is doubtful whether the content is true, the author claims responsibility, so we will disclose it for now." "The aforementioned situation, if not fabricated," is because the gentleman is also suspicious and cautious in his words! However, rumors confuse the public and concern the reputation of the school, so our school cannot remain silent. I am providing a brief description of the actual situation and asking your publication to disclose a correction (omission). This is addressed to Mr. Han of the Women's Section of the Shenbao Newspaper, Qingdao Municipal Girls' Middle School, May 18th.

Editor's note: The editor of this publication is not surnamed Han, and it is unknown to whom "Mr. Han" refers.

Shaoxing Tea Industry is Depressed 284

Shaoxing Ping Shui Yao Guo Zhen, near the mountains, is an important tea producing area in Zhejiang Province, and the export volume is no less than Suichun. The mountain households in that place, in the years of the Republic of China 78, in view of the sluggish sales of round tea and the difficulty of livelihood, they decided to change the flag tea to seek new ways out. Every time the new tea is listed, tea merchants from Suhanghu and Guangxi bring money to the producing area to search for purchases. For more than ten years, the business has been prosperous. Unfortunately, in recent years, due to the influence of bandits and the collection of various donations and taxes, the buyers from all over the world have not come forward, so the business has been depressed and almost fallen to the bottom. At present, the tea lines that buy and sell on behalf of customers in that place are also losing money year after year, and the capital is difficult to support. This year, only one or two tea lines are prepared to open in the town, and the market is still quiet and empty, and the scene is quite bleak.

Last year, only one company in the county set up Zhuang to handle tea, and the decline has reached the extreme. Recently, the red bandits in the county have been besieged by the National Army and are gradually being cleared. Tea merchants in the county seat Zhangcun Street Xiaoyushan and other places, in view of the fact that the Shanghai market attaches importance to low Zhuang, the mountain price of the producing area is flat, and the export of boxed tea can be transported by the Hangjiang Railway, and the traffic is more convenient than before. They are all planning to restore the old business. In total, there are nine Zhuang numbers that have been opened this year, and there are about three or four that are brewing to be completed, and the market suddenly presents a picture of revival.
